'\nBest Regards,\nBrad\n_______________________________________\nUnstrung Inc. Announces The Unstrung 25\nURL(s): www.unstrung.com\nNEW YORK, May 22, 2001--Unstrung Inc. publisher of Unstrung\n(www.unstrung.com), a leading publication for the wireless industry,\nrevealed the winners of this year\'s Unstrung 25 Most Innovative Wireless\nCompanies.\nThe Unstrung 25 celebrates the spirit of being unstrung - being tied to\nnothing but the future, daring to innovate and be different - and companies\nthat Unstrung believes are going to be profitable. The winners were\nannounced today by Josh Newman, founder and editor, Unstrung Inc.\nThe winners of this year\'s Unstrung 25 Most Innovative Wireless Companies\nare: Mobliss (Seattle, WA); Stick Networks (Dallas, TX); ViAir (Seattle,\nWA); Stellcom (San Diego, CA); Schema (Israel); Mspect (Sunnyvale, CA);\nSEVEN (Redwood City, CA); Lutris (Santa Cruz, CA); PrarieComm (Rolling\nMeadows, IL); Digital Bridges (Scotland); Brience (San Francisco, CA);\nGravitate (South San Francisco, CA); BitFlash (Ottawa, Canada); Wireless\nServices (Bellevue, WA); Radio Frame (Redmond, WA); TCS (Annapolis, MD);\nSkycross (Maitland, FL); Compaq (Houston, TX); Upoc (New York, NY); 724\nSolutions (Toronto, Ontario); Vaultus (New York, NY); ViaFone (Redwood City,\nCA); Mobilocity (New York, NY); Wysdom (Toronto, Ontario); and FusionOne\n(San Jose, CA).\n"I\'d like to congratulate this year\'s Unstrung 25. We are very excited about\nthis year\'s members," reveals Newman. "At Unstrung we like to get to know a\ncompany, not just for what they do, but for who\'s behind it and this latest\ngroup is a formidable assemblage of wireless industry innovators, thinkers\nand leaders. I look forward to watching them continue to make strides within\nthe industry over the course of the year."\nThe Unstrung editorial staff evaluated over 1500 companies over the course\nof the year, speaking with CEO\'s, CTO\'s and employees at each of the\nnominated companies. The winners of the Unstrung 25 were chosen based upon\nthe following criteria:\n- Vision - The companies demonstrate a clarity of vision and, an\nunderstanding of the marketplace that allows them to take advantage of every\nopportunity.\n- Money - The companies will either get funding, become profitable, or get\nbought before the end of the year.\n- Innovation - The companies have found a new way to get at the problem of\nmobilizing a nation.\n- Competition - The companies stand out not only against the industry as a\nwhole, but also against the competition.\n- Management - The CEO\'s and executive management must have a proven\ncollective track record. But, more importantly they demonstrate an\naggressive, forward-thinking outlook of the wireless industry and the poise\nto execute the company\'s innovations and spirit.\nTo demonstrate the impact and foresight of the Unstrung 25, after the\nwinners were announced last year, the members of the Unstrung 25 had a\nspectacular year despite the state of the industry as a whole. Tantau was\nbought for $380 million. Xypoint was picked up for close to $100 million.\nNomadIQ was acquired for $30 million. Leap Wireless tripled its subscriber\nbase. ViaFone received over $20 million in funding. FusionOne garnered $80\nmillion. Upoc took $18 million. 724 Solutions\' revenue was up over 300% from\nlast year. Savos was obtained for an undisclosed amount. GEO Interactive\ntotaled $30 million in sales.\n"The wireless market is as crowded as ever and there\'s a lot of money thrown\ninto companies that are running on blind hope that if you build it they will\ncome," says Bill Martin, chief executive officer, Unstrung Inc. "The\nUnstrung 25 differ in that they posses the knowledge, understanding, and\nconfidence in the marketplace that allows them to take advantage of every\nopportunity.
